<p>The <b>Beijing-Tibet Expressway</b> (<a href="/wiki/Chinese_language" title="Chinese language">Chinese</a>: <span lang="zh">北京－西藏高速公路</span>; <a href="/wiki/Pinyin" title="Pinyin">pinyin</a>: <i><span lang="zh-Latn-pinyin">Běijīng－Xīzàng gāosù gōnglù</span></i>), commonly abbreviated to <b>Jingzang Expressway</b> (<a href="/wiki/Chinese_language" title="Chinese language">Chinese</a>: <span lang="zh">京藏高速</span>), also known as <b>Beijing-Lhasa Expressway</b> (<b>Jingla Expressway</b>; <a href="/wiki/Chinese_language" title="Chinese language">Chinese</a>: <span lang="zh">京拉高速公路</span>) or <b>China National Expressway 6</b>, is part of the <a href="/wiki/Expressways_of_China" title="Expressways of China">Chinese national expressway network</a> and is planned to connect the nation's capital, <a href="/wiki/Beijing" title="Beijing">Beijing</a>, to the capital of the <a href="/wiki/Tibet_Autonomous_Region" title="Tibet Autonomous Region">Tibet Autonomous Region</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lhasa_(prefecture-level_city)" title="Lhasa (prefecture-level city)">Lhasa</a>.
</p><p>It passes through a total of seven <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Administrative_divisions_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Administrative divisions of the People's Republic of China">China's administrative regions</a>, including the Beijing municipality, the province of <a href="/wiki/Hebei" title="Hebei">Hebei</a>, the autonomous regions of <a href="/wiki/Inner_Mongolia" title="Inner Mongolia">Inner Mongolia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ningxia" title="Ningxia">Ningxia</a>, the provinces of <a href="/wiki/Gansu" title="Gansu">Gansu</a> and <a href="/wiki/Qinghai" title="Qinghai">Qinghai</a>, and finally the <a href="/wiki/Tibet_Autonomous_Region" title="Tibet Autonomous Region">Tibet Autonomous Region</a>.
</p>

</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Passage">Passage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=G6_Beijing%E2%80%93Lhasa_Expressway&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Passage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="center"><div class="thumb tnone"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:G6_expressway_from_offramp_to_North_Fifth_Ring_Road,_Beijing.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2376" data-file-width="5587" decoding="async" height="128" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/G6_expressway_from_offramp_to_North_Fifth_Ring_Road%2C_Beijing.jpg/300px-G6_expressway_from_offramp_to_North_Fifth_Ring_Road%2C_Beijing.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/G6_expressway_from_offramp_to_North_Fifth_Ring_Road%2C_Beijing.jpg/450px-G6_expressway_from_offramp_to_North_Fifth_Ring_Road%2C_Beijing.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/G6_expressway_from_offramp_to_North_Fifth_Ring_Road%2C_Beijing.jpg/600px-G6_expressway_from_offramp_to_North_Fifth_Ring_Road%2C_Beijing.jpg 2x" width="300"/></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:G6_expressway_from_offramp_to_North_Fifth_Ring_Road,_Beijing.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>G6 Expressway at the interchange with the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fifth_Ring_Road" title="Fifth Ring Road">Fifth Ring Road</a> in northern Beijing.</div></div></div></div>
<p>Beginning from Beijing and driving southwest to Lhasa, The expressway runs approximately 3,710 kilometres (2,310 miles) through Hebei, Inner Mongolia, Ningxia, Gansu and Qinghai, for a total of seven provincial-level divisions.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title='is this just regurgitating what was said earlier about "administrative divisions"? (August 2010)'>clarification needed</span></a></i>]</sup>  Excluding the two terminal points, it passes through the major cities of <a href="/wiki/Zhangjiakou" title="Zhangjiakou">Zhangjiakou</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jining_District" title="Jining District">Jining District</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hohhot" title="Hohhot">Hohhot</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bayannur" title="Bayannur">Bayannur</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wuhai" title="Wuhai">Wuhai</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yinchuan" title="Yinchuan">Yinchuan</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wuzhong_City" title="Wuzhong City">Wuzhong</a>, <a href="/wiki/Baiyin" title="Baiyin">Baiyin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lanzhou" title="Lanzhou">Lanzhou</a>, <a href="/wiki/Xining" title="Xining">Xining</a> and <a href="/wiki/Golmud" title="Golmud">Golmud</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title="unordered list. is this heading in the direction from beijing? needs to be clear (August 2010)">clarification needed</span></a></i>]</sup>
</p><p>As of August 2010, just over fifty percent of the expressway is open to traffic, which mainly comprises the stretch between Beijing and Xining. Like <a href="/wiki/China_National_Highway_109" title="China National Highway 109">China National Highway 109</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Qingzang_railway" title="Qingzang railway">Qingzang railway</a>, it is expected to pass west through Golmud before heading southwest into Tibet and Lhasa. Because of climatic conditions, this stretch of the expressway does not yet have a construction timetable.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p><p>As of 2019 the expressway is completed between Beijing and Golmud, and the section between Nagqu and Lhasa has begun construction. The mountainous section between Golmud and Nagqu is not yet shown on maps.
</p><p>The G6 merges with the <a href="/wiki/G7_Beijing%E2%80%93%C3%9Cr%C3%BCmqi_Expressway" title="G7 Beijing–Ürümqi Expressway">G7</a> in Huhhot and does not split until Linhe(now Baynnur).
</p>

<ul><li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Beijing-Pinggu-Jizhou_Expressway&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Beijing-Pinggu-Jizhou Expressway (page does not exist)">S3201 Beijing-Pinggu-Jizhou</a></li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Jingjin_Expressway&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Jingjin Expressway (page does not exist)">S3301 Second Beijing-Tianjin Corridor</a></li>
<li><i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Beijing_Lixian_Airport_Expressway&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Beijing Lixian Airport Expressway (page does not exist)">S3501 Expressway for 2nd Airport</a></i></li>
<li><i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Beijing-Yuxian_Expressway&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Beijing-Yuxian Expressway (page does not exist)">S3701 Beijing-Yuxian</a></i></li>
<li><i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Beijing-Chongli_Expressway&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Beijing-Chongli Expressway (page does not exist)">S3801 Beijing-Chongli</a></i></li>
<li><i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Northern_Beijing_2nd_Airport_Line&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Northern Beijing 2nd Airport Line (page does not exist)">S3300 Northern 2nd Airport</a></i></li>
<li><i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Beijing-Xiong%27an_Expressway&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Beijing-Xiong'an Expressway (page does not exist)">Beijing-Xiong'an</a></i></li></ul>
</div></td></tr><tr><th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="width:11em">Local Expressways</th><td class="navbox-list navbox-odd hlist" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;padding:0px"><div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
